b'# --------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n# ------------  Metody Systemowe i Decyzyjne w Informatyce  ----------------\r\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n#  Zadanie 4: Zadanie zaliczeniowe\r\n#  autorzy: A. Gonczarek, J. Kaczmar, S. Zareba\r\n#  2017\r\n# --------------------------------------------------------------------------\r\n\r\nimport pickle as pkl\r\nimport numpy as np\r\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\r\nimport time\r\n\r\nN_CLASSES = 36\r\n\r\nDEF_K = np.arange(1, 201, 2)\r\n\r\ndef hamming_distance(X, X_train):\r\n    """\r\n    :param X: zbior porownwanych obiektow N1xD\r\n    :param X_train: zbior obiektow do ktorych porownujemy N2xD\r\n    Funkcja wyznacza odleglosci Hamminga obiektow ze zbioru X od\r\n    obiektow X_train. Odleglosci obiektow z jednego i drugiego\r\n    zbioru zwrocone zostana w postaci macierzy\r\n    :return: macierz odleglosci pomiedzy obiektami z X i X_train N1xN2\r\n    """\r\n    A = (1 - X) @ X_train.T\r\n    B = (1 - X_train) @ X.T\r\n\r\n    return A + B.T\r\n\r\n\r\ndef sort_train_labels_knn(Dist, y):\r\n    """\r\n    Funkcja sortujaca etykiety klas danych treningowych y\r\n    wzgledem prawdopodobienstw zawartych w macierzy Dist.\r\n    Funkcja zwraca macierz o wymiarach N1xN2. W kazdym\r\n    wierszu maja byc posortowane etykiety klas z y wzgledem\r\n    wartosci podobienstw odpowiadajacego wiersza macierzy\r\n    Dist\r\n    :param Dist: macierz odleglosci pomiedzy obiektami z X\r\n    i X_train N1xN2\r\n    :param y: wektor etykiet o dlugosci N2\r\n    :return: macierz etykiet klas posortowana wzgledem\r\n    wartosci podobienstw odpowiadajacego wiersza macierzy\r\n    Dist. Uzyc algorytmu mergesort.\r\n    """\r\n    A = np.argsort(Dist, 1, \'mergesort\')\r\n    return y[A]\r\n\r\n\r\ndef p_y_x_knn(y, k):\r\n    """\r\n    Funkcja wyznacza rozklad prawdopodobienstwa p(y|x) dla\r\n    kazdej z klas dla obiektow ze zbioru testowego wykorzystujac\r\n    klasfikator KNN wyuczony na danych trenningowych\r\n    :param y: macierz posortowanych etykiet dla danych treningowych N1xN2\r\n    :param k: liczba najblizszuch sasiadow dla KNN\r\n    :return: macierz prawdopodobienstw dla obiektow z X\r\n    """\r\n    y = y[:, :k]\r\n    res = []\r\n    for row in y:\r\n        res.append(np.bincount(row, minlength=N_CLASSES))\r\n    res = np.array(res)\r\n    return res/k\r\n\r\n\r\ndef classification_error(p_y_x, y_true):\r\n    """\r\n    Wyznacz blad klasyfikacji.\r\n    :param p_y_x: macierz przewidywanych prawdopodobienstw\r\n    :param y_true: zbior rzeczywistych etykiet klas 1xN.\r\n    Kazdy wiersz macierzy reprezentuje rozklad p(y|x)\r\n    :return: blad klasyfikacji\r\n    """\r\n    p_y_x_rev = np.flip(p_y_x, 1)\r\n    preds = np.shape(p_y_x)[1] - 1 - np.argmax(p_y_x_rev, 1)\r\n    n = np.shape(p_y_x)[0]\r\n    return np.sum(preds != y_true) / n\r\n\r\n\r\ndef model_selection_knn(Xval, Xtrain, yval, ytrain, k_values):\r\n    """\r\n    :param Xval: zbior danych walidacyjnych N1xD\r\n    :param Xtrain: zbior danych treningowych N2xD\r\n    :param yval: etykiety klas dla danych walidacyjnych 1xN1\r\n    :param ytrain: etykiety klas dla danych treningowych 1xN2\r\n    :param k_values: wartosci parametru k, ktore maja zostac sprawdzone\r\n    :return: funkcja wykonuje selekcje modelu knn i zwraca krotke (best_error,best_k,errors), gdzie best_error to najnizszy\r\n    osiagniety blad, best_k - k dla ktorego blad byl najnizszy, errors - lista wartosci bledow dla kolejnych k z k_values\r\n    """\r\n    start = time.time()\r\n    distance = hamming_distance(Xval, Xtrain)\r\n    print(np.shape(distance))\r\n    sorted_labels = np.squeeze(sort_train_labels_knn(distance, ytrain))\r\n    print(np.shape(sorted_labels))\r\n    p = p_y_x_knn(sorted_labels, k_values[0])\r\n    print(time.time() - start)\r\n    best_error = classification_error(p, yval)\r\n    best_k = k_values[0]\r\n    errors = []\r\n\r\n    for k in k_values:\r\n        print(k)\r\n        p = p_y_x_knn(sorted_labels, k)\r\n        error = classification_error(p, yval)\r\n        print(error)\r\n        errors.append(error)\r\n        if(error < best_error):\r\n            best_error = error\r\n            best_k = k\r\n    return (best_error, best_k, errors)\r\n\r\n\r\ndef feature_extraction(X):\r\n    X = np.reshape(X, (-1, 56, 56))\r\n    res = []\r\n    for image in X:\r\n        features = []\r\n        for i in range(8):\r\n            for k in range(8):\r\n                a = image[i * 7:i * 7 + 7, k * 7:k * 7 + 7]\r\n                features.append(np.mean(a))\r\n        res.append(features)\r\n    return np.array(res)\r\n\r\n\r\ndef absolute_distance(X, X_train):\r\n    res = []\r\n    for im1 in X:\r\n        diffs = []\r\n        for im2 in X_train:\r\n            diffs.append(np.sum(np.abs(im1 - im2)))\r\n        res.append(diffs)\r\n    return np.array(res)\r\n\r\ndef predict(x):\r\n    """\r\n    Funkcja pobiera macierz przykladow zapisanych w macierzy X o wymiarach NxD i zwraca wektor y o wymiarach Nx1,\r\n    gdzie kazdy element jest z zakresu {0, ..., 35} i oznacza znak rozpoznany na danym przykladzie.\r\n    :param x: macierz o wymiarach NxD\r\n    :return: wektor o wymiarach Nx1\r\n    """\r\n    pass\r\n\r\n\r\nif __name__ == \'__main__\':\r\n    with open("train.pkl", \'rb\') as file:\r\n        data = pkl.load(file)\r\n    X = data[0]\r\n    Y = data[1]\r\n    x_train = X[:18000, :]\r\n    y_train = Y[:18000, :]\r\n    x_val = X[18000:20500, :]\r\n    y_val = Y[18000:20500, :]\r\n\r\n    a = feature_extraction(x_train)\r\n    start = time.time()\r\n    b = feature_extraction(x_val)\r\n    dist = absolute_distance(a, b)\r\n    print(time.time() - start)\r\n    # best_error, best_k, errors = model_selection_knn(x_val, x_train, y_val, y_train, DEF_K)\r\n    # print(f"best error: {best_error}, best k: {best_k}")\r\n    # print(errors)'

b'\r\n#include "strend.h"\r\n#include <stdio.h>\r\n\r\n/* int main() executes strendTest() */\r\nvoid strendTest() {\r\n\t// something to search for\r\n\tchar text1[99] = "Hello there";\r\n\tchar text2[99] = "there";\r\n\t\r\n\t// Executing the function, and see what we get..\r\n\tif(testText(text1, text2)) {\r\n\t\tprintf("Found text \'%s\' at the end of \'%s\'\\n", text2, text1);\r\n\t} else {\r\n\t\tprintf("Could not find \'%s\' at the end of \'%s\'\\n", text2, text1);\r\n\t}\r\n}\r\n\r\nint testText(char *text1, char *text2) {\r\n\tint n,m,b = 0;\r\n\tchar *editText1,*editText2;\r\n\teditText1 = text1;\r\n\teditText2 = text2;\r\n\tfor(n=0; *editText1 != \'\\0\'; *editText1++) {\r\n\t\t/* strlen(text1) */\r\n \t\tn++;\r\n\t}\r\n\tfor(m=0; *editText2 != \'\\0\'; *editText2++) {\r\n\t\t/* strlen(text2) */\r\n\t\tm++;\r\n\t}\r\n\tfor(;n != 0; --n) {\r\n\t\t/* looping text1 to compare chars  */\r\n\t\tif(n <= m && *(editText1-n) == *(editText2-n)) {\r\n\t\t\t/* will be TRUE where text2 _should_ begin in text1 (the end), and */\r\n\t\t\t/* comparing text2[0] and forward against text1[n] and forward */\r\n\t\t\t\r\n\t\t\t/* increasing b to see if it\'s matching */\r\n\t\t\tb++;\r\n\t\t\tif(m == b) {\r\n\t\t\t\t/* if all the word\'s match, we\'re found our word! exit function! */\r\n\t\t\t\treturn 1;\r\n\t\t\t}\r\n\t\t}\r\n\t}\r\n\t/* Didn\'t find every chars at the end of the sentence. exit function! */\r\n\treturn 0;\r\n}'

b'void afisare(int a[], int n) {\n    int i;\n    \n    for (i = 0; i < n; i++)\n        printf("%d ", a[i]);\n        \n    printf("\\n")\n}\n\nvoid combinari(int a[], int n, int p) {\n    if (n == p) {\n        afisare(a, n);\n    } else {\n        int i;\n        \n        for (i = p; i < n; i++) {\n            int tmp = a[p];\n            a[p] = a[i];\n            a[i] = tmp;\n            combinari(a, n, p+1);\n            a[i] = a[p];\n            a[p] = tmp; \n        }\n    }\n}\n\nvoid aranjamente(int a[], int n, int k, int p) {\n    if (n == p) {\n        afisare(a, n);\n    } else {\n        int i;\n        \n        for (i = 0; i < k; i++) {\n            a[p] += i;\n            aranjamente(a, n, p+1);\n            a[p] -= i;\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nint a[3] = {1, 2, 3};\ncombinari(a,3,0);\n\nint b[3] = { 1, 1, 1};\naranjamente(a, 3, 5, 0);'

b'# Self Signed SSL Certificate for AWS ALB\n\n1. Generate private key\n\n    ```bash\n    $> openssl genrsa 2048 > my-private-key.pem\n    ```\n\n2. Generate certificate using private key, you will be prompted to fill some fields. Fill required fields randomly, except for `Common Name` fill it with `*.amazonaws.com` or your valid domain name\n\n    ```bash\n    $> openssl -req -new -x509 -nodes -sha256 -days 365 -key my-private-key.pem -outform PEM -out my-certificate.pem\n    ```\n\n3. Upload certificate & its private key to Amazon Certificate Manager\n\n    ```bash\n    $> aws acm import-certificate --certificate file://my-certificate.pem --private-key file://my-private-key.pem\n    ```\n4. Certificate should now show up in AWS Console for ALB'

b'function VIP( player, duration )\r\n{\r\nlocal g_time, duration_type;\r\n\r\nswitch( duration.len() )\r\n{\r\n\r\ncase 2:\r\ng_time = duration.slice(0.1);\r\nbreak;\r\n\r\ncase 3:\r\ng_time = duration.slice(2.3);\r\nbreak;\r\ndefault:\r\nMessagePlayer("Invalid duration", player );\r\n}\r\n\r\nlocal g_time, g_duration_type_;\r\n\r\nswitch( duration_type )\r\n{\r\ncase "d":\r\ng_time_ = g_time.tointeger() * 86400;\r\ng_duration_type_ = "day(s)";\r\nbreak;\r\n\r\ndefault:\r\nMessagePlayer("Invalid format", player );\r\n}\r\n\r\nif ( g_time.tointeger() > 0 )\r\n{\r\nlocal cost = g_time.tointeger() * 30000;\r\nif ( player.Cash >= cost )\r\n{\r\nlocal dur = g_time + " " + g_duration_type_;\r\nMessagePlayer("Bought VIP "+cost+" expires after "+dur, player );\r\nQuerySQL(db, "INSERT INTO VIPs ( Name, Time, TimeExpire ) VALUES ( \'"+player.Name+"\', \'"+time()+"\', \'"+g_time+"\'" );\r\nDecCash( player, cost );\r\nstats[player.ID].VIP = true;\r\nstats[player.ID].VIPExp = g_time;\r\n}\r\nelse MessagePlayer("Need "+cost+" to buy VIP for "+g_time+" days", player );\r\n}\r\nelse MessagePlayer("Please add days more than 0 to buy vip", player );\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction CheckVIP( player )\r\n{\r\nlocal q = QuerySQL( db, "SELECT * FROM VIPs WHERE Name=\'"+player.Name+"\'");\r\nif (GetSQLColumnData(q,0))\r\n{\r\nstats[player.ID].VIP = true;\r\nstats[player.ID].VIPExp = GetSQLColumnData(q,2);\r\n}\r\nFreeSQLQuery(q);\r\n}\r\n\r\nfunction Duration( secs )\r\n{\r\nlocal nDays, nHours, nMinutes, nMonths, nYears, nTime = "";\r\nnYears = secs/31536000;\r\nsecs = secs%31536000;\r\nnMonths = secs/2678400;\r\nsecs = secs%2678400;\r\nnDays = secs/86400;\r\nsecs = secs%86400;\r\nnHours = secs/3600;\r\nsecs = secs%3600;\r\nnMinutes = secs/60;\r\nsecs = secs%60;\r\nif( nYears != 0 ) nTime = nTime + nYears + " Year" + (nYears > 1 ? "s":"");\r\nif( nMonths != 0 ) nTime = nTime + (nTime != "" ? ", ":"") + nMonths + " month" + (nMonths > 1 ? "s":"");\r\nif( nDays != 0 ) nTime = nTime  + (nTime != "" ? ", ":"") + nDays + " day" + (nDays > 1 ? "s":"");\r\nif( nHours != 0 ) nTime = nTime + (nTime != "" ? ", ":"") + nHours + " hour" + (nHours > 1 ? "s":"");\r\nif( nMinutes != 0 ) nTime = nTime +  (nTime != "" ? ", ":"") + nMinutes + " min" + (nMinutes > 1 ? "s":"");\r\nif( secs != 0 ) nTime = nTime + (nTime != "" ? " and ":"") + secs + " sec" + (secs > 1 ? "s":"");\r\nreturn nTime;\r\n}\r\n\r\n\r\nfunction onPlayerCommand( player, command, text )\r\n{\r\n\r\nelse if ( cmd == "buyvip" )\r\n{\r\nif ( !text ) Syntax_MSG("/"+cmd+" <days>", player );\r\nelse if ( stats[player.ID].VIP == true ) Error_MSG("You are already a VIP", player);\r\nelse{\r\nlocal duration = GetTok( text, " ", 1);\r\nif (!duration) Syntax_MSG("/"+cmd+" <days>", player );\r\nelse{\r\nVIP( player, duration );\r\n}\r\n}\r\n}'

b'1)  In JavaScript, there are two types of scope: Local Scope, and Global Scope. Each function creates a new scope that determines the accessiblity and visibility of the variables. Variables defined inside a function are not visible from outside the function. Variables declared within a function become local to a function and therefor have local scope, meaning they can only be accessed within the function. On the other hand, when a variable is declared outside a function it becomes global. A global variable has global scope, meaning all scripts and functions on a webpage can access it.\n2)  It is important to declare your variables because if you don\'t, they become global. Global variables should be avoided, unless explicitly necessary, because they can create unintended side effects that render your code indeterminate. Other potential problems include limiting your code to being used only once in any given context, easily conflicting with the work of other programmers, and slower performance since local scopes are typically located first.\n3) When using "Strict Mode," global variables are not automatically created. Strict mode is declared at the beginning of the fuction, giving it either local or global scope. This makes it easier to write secure JavaScript because it changes previously accepted bad syntax into real errors.\n4)  A side effect is caused in global variables when a function reaches outside its local scope into a parent scope and alters a value that lives there. A pure function is a function which given the same output with no side effects. You can tell a function is impure when it makes sense to call it without using its return value. It\'s a good idea to favor pure functions because they are the simplest reusable building blocks of code.'

b'#coding=utf-8\r\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\r\nimport matplotlib.lines as lines\r\nimport numpy as np\r\nimport random\r\n\r\n\r\ndef cats_steps(xi, yi):\r\n    n = 23\r\n    m = 2\r\n    cats = [0] * n\r\n    k = 0\r\n    for i in range(n):\r\n        cats[i] = [0] * m\r\n\r\n    for i in range (-1, 2):\r\n        for j in range (-1, 2):\r\n            cats[k][0] = xi + i\r\n            cats[k][1] = yi + j\r\n            k = k + 1\r\n    for i in range (-3, 4):\r\n        cats[k][0] = xi\r\n        cats[k][1] = yi + i\r\n        k = k + 1\r\n\r\n    for i in range (-3, 4):\r\n        cats[k][0] = xi + i\r\n        cats[k][1] = yi\r\n        k = k + 1\r\n    return cats\r\n\r\ndef mouse_steps(xi, yi):\r\n    n = 10\r\n    m = 2\r\n    mouse = [0] * n\r\n    k = 0\r\n    for i in range(n):\r\n        mouse[i] = [0] * m\r\n\r\n    for i in range (-2, 3):\r\n        mouse[k][0] = xi\r\n        mouse[k][1] = yi + i\r\n        k = k + 1\r\n\r\n    for i in range (-2, 3):\r\n        mouse[k][0] = xi + i\r\n        mouse[k][1] = yi\r\n        k = k + 1\r\n    return mouse\r\n\r\n\r\ndef distance(x0, x1, y0, y1):\r\n    return np.sqrt(np.square(x1-x0)+np.square(y1-y0))\r\n\r\n\r\ndef find_min_distance(x0, x1, y0, y1):\r\n    steps = cats_steps(x0, y0)\r\n    # print steps\r\n    distances = find_distances(x1, y1, steps)\r\n    # print distances\r\n    min_dist = min(distances)\r\n    min_dist_idx = [i for i, v in enumerate(distances) if v == min_dist]\r\n    # print min_dist_idx\r\n    random_idx = random.choice(min_dist_idx)\r\n    return steps[random_idx][0], steps[random_idx][1]\r\n\r\n\r\ndef find_max_cat_steps(x0, y0, steps):\r\n    cat_steps = []\r\n    cat_curr = x0, y0\r\n    step_count = 0;\r\n    for i in steps:\r\n        # print "search for " + str(i) + " cat at " + str(x0) + " " + str(y0)\r\n        while cat_curr != tuple(i):\r\n            cat_curr = find_min_distance(cat_curr[0], i[0], cat_curr[1], i[1])\r\n            step_count += 1\r\n            # print str(tuple(cat_curr)) + " " + str(tuple(i))\r\n        cat_steps.append(step_count)\r\n        step_count = 0\r\n    # print cat_steps\r\n    max_cat_step = max(cat_steps)\r\n    max_cat_idx = [i for i, v in enumerate(cat_steps) if v == max_cat_step]\r\n    random_idx = random.choice(max_cat_idx)\r\n    return steps[random_idx][0], steps[random_idx][1]\r\n\r\n\r\ndef find_min_cat_steps(x0, y0, steps):\r\n    cat_steps = []\r\n    cat_curr = x0, y0\r\n    step_count = 0;\r\n    for i in steps:\r\n        # print "search for " + str(i) + " cat at " + str(x0) + " " + str(y0)\r\n        while cat_curr != tuple(i):\r\n            cat_curr = find_min_distance(cat_curr[0], i[0], cat_curr[1], i[1])\r\n            step_count += 1\r\n            # print str(tuple(cat_curr)) + " " + str(tuple(i))\r\n        cat_steps.append(step_count)\r\n        step_count = 0\r\n    # print cat_steps\r\n    max_cat_step = min(cat_steps)\r\n    max_cat_idx = [i for i, v in enumerate(cat_steps) if v == max_cat_step]\r\n    random_idx = random.choice(max_cat_idx)\r\n    return steps[random_idx][0], steps[random_idx][1]\r\n\r\ndef find_max_distance(x0, x1, y0, y1):\r\n    steps = mouse_steps(x1, y1)\r\n    # b'use std::io::{self, Read};\nuse std::str::{Lines};\n\nfn decode(word : &str) -> (i32, i32) {\n    let mut x: i32 = 0;\n    let mut y: i32 = 0;\n    \n    for (i, ch) in word.bytes().enumerate() {\n        let c = ch as i32;\n        x |= c & (1 << i);\n        y |= if c & ( 1 << ((3+i) % 6 )) != 0 {\n            (1 << i)\n        } else {\n            0\n        }\n    }\n\n    (x, y)\n}\n\nfn lookup(word: &str, (x, y) : (i32, i32)) -> String {\n    let bs : Vec<u8> = word.bytes().collect();\n    let ch1: u8 = bs[x as usize];\n    let ch2: u8 = bs[y as usize];\n\n    let v = vec![ch1, ch2];\n\n    std::str::from_utf8(&v).unwrap().to_string()\n}\n\nfn process(lines: &mut Lines) {\n    let _n = lines\n        .next()\n        .map(|s : &str| s.parse::<i32>());\n\n    if _n.is_some() {\n        let p = lines.next().unwrap().split(" ").map(decode);\n        let s = lines.next().unwrap();\n\n        let r : Vec<String> = p.map(|i| lookup(s, i)).collect();\n        println!("{}", r.join(""));\n        match lines.next() {\n            None => (),\n            Some(_) => process(lines),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn main() {\n    let mut buffer = String::new();\n\n    io::stdin().read_to_string(&mut buffer).unwrap();\n\n    let mut lines = buffer.lines();\n    lines.next();\n    process(&mut lines);\n}'

b'#ifndef VPVIEW__H\r\n#define VPVIEW__H\r\n\r\n#include <algorithm>\r\n#include <iterator>\r\n#include <vector>\r\n\r\nclass DummyPredicate {};\r\n\r\ntemplate <class T> class vecs_view {\r\n  typedef typename std::vector<T>::iterator vecit;\r\n\r\nprotected:\r\n  std::vector<T> &fr;\r\n  std::vector<T> &sr;\r\n\r\npublic:\r\n  vecs_view(std::vector<T> &a, std::vector<T> &b) : fr(a), sr(b) {}\r\n\r\n  int size() const { return fr.size() + sr.size(); }\r\n\r\n  void negate() { fr.swap(sr); }\r\n\r\n  class iterator : public std::iterator<std::bidirectional_iterator_tag, T> {\r\n\r\n    vecit curr;\r\n    vecit end;\r\n    vecit next;\r\n\r\n    void inc() {\r\n      ++curr;\r\n      if (curr == end) {\r\n        curr = next;\r\n      }\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    void dec() {\r\n      if (curr == next) {\r\n        curr = end;\r\n      }\r\n      --curr;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n  public:\r\n    iterator(vecit c, vecit e, vecit n) : curr(c), end(e), next(n) {}\r\n\r\n    iterator &operator++() {\r\n      inc();\r\n      return *this;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    iterator operator++(int) {\r\n      iterator ret = *this;\r\n      inc();\r\n      return ret;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    iterator &operator--() {\r\n      dec();\r\n      return *this;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    iterator operator--(int) {\r\n      iterator ret = *this;\r\n      dec();\r\n      return ret;\r\n    }\r\n\r\n    bool operator==(const iterator &it) const { return curr == it.curr; }\r\n\r\n    bool operator!=(const iterator &it) const { return !(*this == it); }\r\n\r\n    T &operator*() const { return *curr; }\r\n  };\r\n\r\n  iterator begin() { return iterator(fr.begin(), fr.end(), sr.begin()); }\r\n\r\n  iterator end() { return iterator(sr.end(), fr.end(), sr.begin()); }\r\n};\r\n\r\ntemplate <class T, class Pred = DummyPredicate>\r\nstruct vectors_predicate_view : vecs_view<T> {\r\n\r\n  vectors_predicate_view(std::vector<T> &a, std::vector<T> &b)\r\n      : vecs_view<T>(a, b), fo(a), so(b) {\r\n    this->fr.insert(this->fr.end(), this->sr.begin(), this->sr.end());\r\n    this->sr = this->fr;\r\n\r\n    this->fr.erase(\r\n        std::remove_if(this->fr.begin(), this->fr.end(), std::not1(Pred())),\r\n        this->fr.end());\r\n    this->sr.erase(std::remove_if(this->sr.begin(), this->sr.end(), Pred()),\r\n                   this->sr.end());\r\n  }\r\n\r\n  ~vectors_predicate_view() {\r\n    this->fr = fo;\r\n    this->sr = so;\r\n  }\r\n\r\nprivate:\r\n  std::vector<T> fo;\r\n  std::vector<T> so;\r\n};\r\n\r\ntemplate <class T>\r\nstruct vectors_predicate_view<T, DummyPredicate> : vecs_view<T> {\r\n\r\n  vectors_predicate_view(std::vector<T> &a, std::vector<T> &b)\r\n      : vecs_view<T>(a, b) {}\r\n};\r\n\r\n#endif'
